posted:Posted May 4, 2024
msg:Summary: It's quite standard, no surprises or surprises. I feel that the hardware and software don't quite match the positioning of a five-star hotel; it's not worth it if the price exceeds 600 yuan/room/night.
Location: The hotel is in an awkward location, not in the city center, and the surrounding facilities are average. You need a car to travel conveniently.
Hygiene: The overall hygiene is clean and tidy. But on the way out of the elevator to the room, you can still smell a distinct musty smell (or is it the smell of formaldehyde?).
Room: The area is large enough, but the facilities are average. The toilet has a small flush, but the sound is loud. The bathtub is not big enough.
Restaurant: There are many categories, but they all feel like common things. There are no sunshine pancakes, small cakes, and other must-haves in five-star hotels. I have taken photos of the breakfast on the first day, you can take a look. It's just that there is no feeling of brightening the eyes.
Indoor swimming pool: The water temperature is not high enough, there is no safety guard at the poolside, and there are safety hazards.
Children's playground: This is shabby, right next to the swimming pool, with a small area (less than 20 square meters?), few utensils, and dim light. . .
Child-friendliness: There is no small stool for children in the bathroom, and it is inconvenient for children with low collars to brush their teeth and wash their faces.
Service: Overall, it is quite friendly and professional, and the response speed is fast. The front desk upgraded the room (from a king-size bed room to a deluxe king-size bed room. After checking out, Maggie in the executive lounge on the second floor took the initiative to add WeChat to learn about the experience of this stay.
Price: This time it happened to be May Day, and the price exceeded 900 yuan/room/night, which is seriously uneconomical. According to the hotel's hardware and software configuration, it is not cost-effective to exceed 600 yuan/room/night.
The above is my personal opinion for your reference.
